└─────────────┴───────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="max2" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">max2<a class="headerlink" href="#max2" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Compares two values and returns the larger one.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">max2(a, b)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>a</code>: The first value.</li><li><code>b</code>: The second value.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The greater of <code>a</code> and <code>b</code>. <code>Float64</code>.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT max2(-1, 2)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─max2(-1, 2)─┐
│           2 │
└─────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="min2" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">min2<a class="headerlink" href="#min2" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Compares two values and returns the smaller one.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">min2(a, b)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>a</code>: The first value.</li><li><code>b</code>: The second value.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The lesser of <code>a</code> and <code>b</code>. <code>Float64</code>.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT min2(-1, 2)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─min2(-1, 2)─┐
│          -1 │
└─────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="multiplydecimal" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">multiplyDecimal<a class="headerlink" href="#multiplydecimal" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Multiplies two <code>Decimal</code> values, <code>a</code> and <code>b</code>. The result is a <code>Decimal256</code>. You can optionally specify the <code>result_scale</code> to control the precision of the output. If <code>result_scale</code> is not provided, the maximum scale of the input values is used. This function is slower than the standard <code>multiply</code> function but offers precise control over decimal arithmetic.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">multiplyDecimal(a, b[, result_scale])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>a</code>: The first value. <a href="../data-types/decimal"><code>Decimal</code></a>.</li><li><code>b</code>: The second value. <a href="../data-types/decimal"><code>Decimal</code></a>.</li><li><code>result_scale</code>: (Optional) The desired scale (number of decimal places) for the result. <a href="../data-types/int-uint"><code>Int/UInt</code></a>.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The product of <code>a</code> and <code>b</code> with the specified or inferred scale. <a href="../data-types/decimal"><code>Decimal256</code></a>.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─multiplyDecimal(toDecimal256(-12, 0), toDecimal32(-2.1, 1), 1)─┐
│                                                           25.2 │
└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="differences-compared-to-regular-multiplication" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Differences compared to regular multiplication<a class="headerlink" href="#differences-compared-to-regular-multiplication" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT toDecimal64(-12.647, 3) * toDecimal32(2.1239, 4)
SELECT toDecimal64(-12.647, 3) as a, toDecimal32(2.1239, 4) as b, multiplyDecimal(a, b)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─multiply(toDecimal64(-12.647, 3), toDecimal32(2.1239, 4))─┐
│                                               -26.8609633 │
└───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
┌───────a─┬──────b─┬─multiplyDecimal(toDecimal64(-12.647, 3), toDecimal32(2.1239, 4))─┐
│ -12.647 │ 2.1239 │                                                         -26.8609 │
└─────────┴────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

The result is a <code>Decimal256</code>. You can optionally specify the <code>result_scale</code> to control the precision of the output. If <code>result_scale</code> is not provided, the maximum scale of the input values is used. This function is slower than the standard <code>divide</code> function but offers precise control over decimal arithmetic.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">divideDecimal(a, b[, result_scale])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>a</code>: The dividend. <a href="../data-types/decimal"><code>Decimal</code></a>.</li><li><code>b</code>: The divisor. <a href="../data-types/decimal"><code>Decimal</code></a>.</li><li><code>result_scale</code>: (Optional) The desired scale (number of decimal places) for the result. <a href="../data-types/int-uint"><code>Int/UInt</code></a>.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The quotient of <code>a</code> divided by <code>b</code> with the specified or inferred scale. <a href="../data-types/decimal"><code>Decimal256</code></a>.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" </pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>a</code>: The integer value whose bytes are to be swapped.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The integer with its bytes reversed. The return type is the same as the input type.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">byteSwap(3351772109)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─byteSwap(3351772109)─┐
│           3455829959 │
└──────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>The previous example can be followed in the following manner:</p><ol><li>Convert the base-10 integer to its equivalent hexadecimal format in big-endian format, for example <code>3351772109 -&gt; C7 C7 FB CD (4 bytes)</code>.</li><li>Reverse the bytes, for example <code>C7 C7 FB CD -&gt; CD FB C7 C7</code>.</li><li>Convert the result back to an integer assuming big-endian, for example <code>CD FB C7 C7  -&gt; 3455829959</code>.</li></ol><p>A use case of this function is reversing IPv4s:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─toIPv4(byteSwap(toUInt32(toIPv4(&#x27;205.251.199.199&#x27;))))─┐
│ 199.199.251.205                                       │
└───────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></article><div class="flex items-center justify-end h-10" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="italic text-caption"><span>Updated<!-- --> \",\"static/chunks/1284-f30446673b9ba073.js\",\"7867\",\"static/chunks/7867-6d0484accd87a171.js\",\"3145\",\"static/chunks/3145-ca0c40eb1bb881d8.js\",\"5107\",\"static/chunks/5107-ef688f2fbbe55825.js\",\"2418\",\"static/chunks/2418-b0d27e6f47546ed6.js\",\"4144\",\"static/chunks/4144-34f98e6e70550e12.js\",\"1147\",\"static/chunks/1147-ac53c80b8f8a3921.js\",\"1749\",\"static/chunks/1749-b2df567f1b8974df.js\",\"5643\",\"static/chunks/5643-5ba78075e5c8bae2.js\",\"1796\",\"static/chunks/1796-b956fe6fe21dbf17.js\",\"787\",\"static/chunks/787-09fc1907ef45c351.js\",\"996\",\"static/chunks/996-ce0ceee74ea8f43a.js\",\"7432\",\"static/chunks/7432-03643de0998568d4.js\",\"5077\",\"static/chunks/app/(sql-reference)/sql-reference/%5B%5B...slug%5D%5D/page-1cd32edffe376f31.js\"],\"default\"]\n21:T612c,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"---\ntitle: Arithmetic Functions reference\nmeta:\n    description: Functions for performing arithmetic operations.\nheadingMaxLevels: 2\n---\n\n# Arithmetic functions\n\nThe following functions are used to perform arithmetic operations.\n\nArithmetic functions work for any two operands of type `UInt8`, `UInt16`, `UInt32`, `UInt64`, `Int8`, `Int16`, `Int32`, `Int64`, `Float32`, or `Float64`.\n\nBefore performing the operation, both operands are cast to the result type. The result type is determined as follows:\n\n- If both operands are up to 32 bits wide, the size of the result type will be the size of the next bigger type following the bigger of the\n  two operands (integer size promotion). For example, `UInt8 + UInt16 = UInt32` or `Float32 * Float32 = Float64`.\n- If one of the operands has 64 or more bits, the size of the result type will be the same size as the bigger of the two operands. For\n  example, `UInt32 + UInt128 = UInt128` or `Float32 * Float64 = Float64`.\n- If one of the operands is signed, the result type will also be signed, otherwise it will be signed. For example, `UInt32 * Int32 = Int64`.\n\nThese rules make sure that the result type will be the smallest type which can represent all possible results. While this introduces a risk\nof overflows around the value range boundary, it ensures that calculations are performed quickly using the maximum native integer width of\n64 bit. This behavior also guarantees compatibility with many other databases which provide 64 bit integers (BIGINT) as the biggest integer\ntype.\n\nFor example:\n\n```sql\nSELECT toTypeName(0), toTypeName(0 + 0), toTypeName(0 + 0 + 0), toTypeName(0 + 0 + 0 + 0)\n```\n\n```text\n┌─toTypeName(0)─┬─toTypeName(plus(0, 0))─┬─toTypeName(plus(plus(0, 0), 0))─┬─toTypeName(plus(plus(plus(0, 0), 0), 0))─┐\n│ UInt8         │ UInt16                 │ UInt32                          │ UInt64                                   │\n└───────────────┴────────────────────────┴─────────────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\nOverflows are produced the same way as in C++.\n\n## plus\n\nCalculates the sum of two numeric values. This function can also add an integer to a Date or DateTime, incrementing days or seconds respectively.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nplus(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The first numeric value, or a Date/DateTime.\n- `b`: The second numeric value, or an integer for Date/DateTime arithmetic.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe sum of `a` and `b`. The return type depends on the input types, following type promotion rules.\n\nAlias: `a + b` (operator)\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT plus(10, 5), 10 + 5, plus(toDate('2023-01-01'), 5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─plus(10, 5)─┬─plus(10, 5)─┬─plus(toDate('2023-01-01'), 5)─┐\n│          15 │          15 │                     2023-01-06 │\n└─────────────┴─────────────┴──────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## minus\n\nCalculates the difference between two numeric values. This function can also subtract an integer from a Date or DateTime, or subtract two Date/DateTime values to get a time difference. The result is always signed.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nminus(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The first numeric value, or a Date/DateTime.\n- `b`: The second numeric value, an integer for Date/DateTime arithmetic, or another Date/DateTime.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe difference between `a` and `b`. The return type depends on the input types, following type promotion rules.\n\nAlias: `a - b` (operator)\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT minus(10, 5), 10 - 5, minus(toDate('2023-01-06'), 5), minus(toDateTime('2023-01-01 10:00:00'), toDateTime('2023-01-01 09:00:00'))\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─minus(10, 5)─┬─minus(10, 5)─┬─minus(toDate('2023-01-06'), 5)─┬─minus(toDateTime('2023-01-01 10:00:00'), toDateTime('2023-01-01 09:00:00'))─┐\n│            5 │            5 │                      2023-01-01 │                                                                       3600 │\n└──────────────┴──────────────┴────────────────────────────────┴────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## multiply\n\nCalculates the product of two numeric values.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nmultiply(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The first numeric value.\n- `b`: The second numeric value.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe product of `a` and `b`. The return type depends on the input types, following type promotion rules.\n\nAlias: `a * b` (operator)\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT multiply(10, 5), 10 * 5, multiply(2.5, 4)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─multiply(10, 5)─┬─multiply(10, 5)─┬─multiply(2.5, 4)─┐\n│              50 │              50 │             10.0 │\n└─────────────────┴─────────────────┴──────────────────┘\n```\n\n## divide\n\nCalculates the quotient of two numeric values. The result type is always `Float64`. For integer division, use `intDiv`. Division by zero results in `inf`, `-inf`, or `nan`.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ndivide(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The dividend.\n- `b`: The divisor.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe quotient of `a` divided by `b`. `Float64`.\n\nAlias: `a / b` (operator)\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT divide(10, 4), 10 / 4, divide(10, 0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─divide(10, 4)─┬─divide(10, 4)─┬─divide(10, 0)─┐\n│           2.5 │           2.5 │           inf │\n└───────────────┴───────────────┴───────────────┘\n```\n\n## intDiv\n\nPerforms integer division, returning the quotient rounded down to the nearest whole number. The result type has the same width as the dividend. This function throws an exception if the divisor is zero, the quotient exceeds the dividend's range, or if dividing the minimum negative number by -1.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nintDiv(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The dividend.\n- `b`: The divisor.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe integer quotient of `a` divided by `b`. The return type matches the width of `a`.\n\n### Example\n\nQuery:\n\n```sql\nSELECT\n    intDiv(toFloat64(1), 0.001) AS res,\n    toTypeName(res)\n```\n\n```result\n┌──res─┬─toTypeName(intDiv(toFloat64(1), 0.001))─┐\n│ 1000 │ Int64                                   │\n└──────┴─────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n```sql\nSELECT\n    intDiv(1, 0.001) AS res,\n    toTypeName(res)\n```\n\n```result\nReceived exception from server (version 23.2.1):\nCode: 153. DB::Exception: Received from localhost:9000. DB::Exception: Cannot perform integer division, because it will produce infinite or too large number: While processing intDiv(1, 0.001) AS res, toTypeName(res). (ILLEGAL_DIVISION)\n```\n\n## intDivOrZero\n\nPerforms integer division similar to `intDiv`, but returns `0` instead of throwing an exception if the divisor is zero or if dividing the minimum negative number by -1.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nintDivOrZero(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The dividend.\n- `b`: The divisor.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe integer quotient of `a` divided by `b`, or `0` in case of division by zero or overflow. The return type matches the width of `a`.\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT intDivOrZero(10, 3), intDivOrZero(10, 0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─intDivOrZero(10, 3)─┬─intDivOrZero(10, 0)─┐\n│                   3 │                   0 │\n└─────────────────────┴─────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## isFinite\n\nChecks if a floating-point number is finite (not infinite and not NaN).\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nisFinite(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The floating-point number to check. `Float32` or `Float64`.\n\n### Returns\n\n`1` if `x` is finite, `0` otherwise. `UInt8`.\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT isFinite(1.0/3.0), isFinite(1.0/0.0), isFinite(0.0/0.0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─isFinite(1 / 3)─┬─isFinite(1 / 0)─┬─isFinite(0 / 0)─┐\n│               1 │               0 │               0 │\n└─────────────────┴─────────────────┴─────────────────┘\n```\n\n## isInfinite\n\nChecks if a floating-point number is infinite.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nisInfinite(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The floating-point number to check. `Float32` or `Float64`.\n\n### Returns\n\n`1` if `x` is infinite, `0` otherwise. `UInt8`. Returns `0` for NaN values.\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT isInfinite(1.0/0.0), isInfinite(-1.0/0.0), isInfinite(0.0/0.0), isInfinite(1.0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─isInfinite(1 / 0)─┬─isInfinite(-1 / 0)─┬─isInfinite(0 / 0)─┬─isInfinite(1)─┐\n│                 1 │                  1 │                 0 │             0 │\n└───────────────────┴────────────────────┴───────────────────┴───────────────┘\n```\n\n## ifNotFinite\n\nReturns the original value if it is finite; otherwise, returns a specified fallback value.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nifNotFinite(x, y)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: Value to check for finiteness. `Float32` or `Float64`.\n- `y`: Fallback value to return if `x` is not finite. `Float32` or `Float64`.\n\n### Returns\n\n`x` if `x` is finite, otherwise `y`. `Float32` or `Float64`.\n\n### Example\n\nQuery:\n\n    SELECT 1/0 as infimum, ifNotFinite(infimum,42)\n\nResult:\n\n    ┌─infimum─┬─ifNotFinite(divide(1, 0), 42)─┐\n    │     inf │                            42 │\n    └─────────┴───────────────────────────────┘\n\nYou can get similar result by using the ternary operator: `isFinite(x) ? x : y`.\n\n## isNaN\n\nChecks if a floating-point number is \"Not a Number\" (NaN).\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nisNaN(x)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `x`: The floating-point number to check. `Float32` or `Float64`.\n\n### Returns\n\n`1` if `x` is NaN, `0` otherwise. `UInt8`.\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT isNaN(0.0/0.0), isNaN(1.0/0.0), isNaN(1.0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─isNaN(0 / 0)─┬─isNaN(1 / 0)─┬─isNaN(1)─┐\n│            1 │            0 │          0 │\n└──────────────┴──────────────┴──────────┘\n```\n\n## modulo\n\nCalculates the remainder of the division of `a` by `b`. The behavior for negative numbers follows C++ semantics (truncated division). An exception is thrown if the divisor is zero or if dividing the minimum negative number by -1.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nmodulo(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The dividend.\n- `b`: The divisor.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe remainder of `a` divided by `b`. The return type is an integer if both inputs are integers, otherwise `Float64`.\n\nAlias: `a % b` (operator)\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT modulo(10, 3), modulo(-10, 3), modulo(10, -3), modulo(-10, -3)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─modulo(10, 3)─┬─modulo(-10, 3)─┬─modulo(10, -3)─┬─modulo(-10, -3)─┐\n│             1 │             -1 │              1 │              -1 │\n└───────────────┴────────────────┴────────────────┴─────────────────┘\n```\n\n## moduloOrZero\n\nCalculates the remainder of the division of `a` by `b`, similar to `modulo`. If the divisor `b` is zero, it returns `0` instead of throwing an exception.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nmoduloOrZero(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The dividend.\n- `b`: The divisor.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe remainder of `a` divided by `b`, or `0` if `b` is zero. The return type is an integer if both inputs are integers, otherwise `Float64`.\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT moduloOrZero(10, 3), moduloOrZero(10, 0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─moduloOrZero(10, 3)─┬─moduloOrZero(10, 0)─┐\n│                   1 │                   0 │\n└─────────────────────┴─────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## positiveModulo\n\nCalculates the remainder of the division of `a` by `b`, always returning a non-negative result. This function is generally slower than `modulo`.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\npositiveModulo(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The dividend.\n- `b`: The divisor.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe non-negative remainder of `a` divided by `b`. The return type is an integer if both inputs are integers, otherwise `Float64`.\n\nAlias:\n- `positive_modulo(a, b)`\n- `pmod(a, b)`\n\n### Example\n\nQuery:\n\n```sql\nSELECT positiveModulo(-1, 10)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─positiveModulo(-1, 10)─┐\n│                      9 │\n└────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## negate\n\nReturns the negative of a numeric value. The result is always signed.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nnegate(a)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The numeric value to negate.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe negated value of `a`. The return type is a signed version of the input type, or the same type if already signed.\n\nAlias: `-a`\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT negate(5), negate(-5), -10\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─negate(5)─┬─negate(-5)─┬─negate(10)─┐\n│        -5 │          5 │         -10 │\n└───────────┴────────────┴────────────┘\n```\n\n## abs\n\nCalculates the absolute value of a numeric input. For unsigned types, it has no effect. For signed types, it returns an unsigned number.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nabs(a)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The numeric value.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe absolute value of `a`. The return type is an unsigned version of the input type if `a` is signed, otherwise the same type.\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT abs(5), abs(-5), abs(0)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─abs(5)─┬─abs(-5)─┬─abs(0)─┐\n│      5 │       5 │      0 │\n└────────┴─────────┴────────┘\n```\n\n## gcd\n\nReturns the greatest common divisor (GCD) of two integer values. An exception is thrown if the divisor is zero or if dividing the minimum negative number by -1.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ngcd(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The first integer.\n- `b`: The second integer.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe greatest common divisor of `a` and `b`. `Int64`.\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT gcd(12, 18), gcd(7, 5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─gcd(12, 18)─┬─gcd(7, 5)─┐\n│           6 │         1 │\n└─────────────┴───────────┘\n```\n\n## lcm\n\nReturns the least common multiple (LCM) of two integer values. An exception is thrown if the divisor is zero or if dividing the minimum negative number by -1.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nlcm(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The first integer.\n- `b`: The second integer.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe least common multiple of `a` and `b`. `Int64`.\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nSELECT lcm(12, 18), lcm(7, 5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─lcm(12, 18)─┬─lcm(7, 5)─┐\n│          36 │        35 │\n└─────────────┴───────────┘\n```\n\n## max2\n\nCompares two values and returns the larger one.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nmax2(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The first value.\n- `b`: The second value.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe greater of `a` and `b`. `Float64`.\n\n### Example\n\nQuery:\n\n```sql\nSELECT max2(-1, 2)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─max2(-1, 2)─┐\n│           2 │\n└─────────────┘\n```\n\n## min2\n\nCompares two values and returns the smaller one.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nmin2(a, b)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The first value.\n- `b`: The second value.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe lesser of `a` and `b`. `Float64`.\n\n### Example\n\nQuery:\n\n```sql\nSELECT min2(-1, 2)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─min2(-1, 2)─┐\n│          -1 │\n└─────────────┘\n```\n\n## multiplyDecimal\n\nMultiplies two `Decimal` values, `a` and `b`. The result is a `Decimal256`. You can optionally specify the `result_scale` to control the precision of the output. If `result_scale` is not provided, the maximum scale of the input values is used. This function is slower than the standard `multiply` function but offers precise control over decimal arithmetic.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nmultiplyDecimal(a, b[, result_scale])\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The first value. [`Decimal`](../data-types/decimal).\n- `b`: The second value. [`Decimal`](../data-types/decimal).\n- `result_scale`: (Optional) The desired scale (number of decimal places) for the result. [`Int/UInt`](../data-types/int-uint).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe product of `a` and `b` with the specified or inferred scale. [`Decimal256`](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Example\n\n```result\n┌─multiplyDecimal(toDecimal256(-12, 0), toDecimal32(-2.1, 1), 1)─┐\n│                                                           25.2 │\n└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### Differences compared to regular multiplication\n\n```sql\nSELECT toDecimal64(-12.647, 3) * toDecimal32(2.1239, 4)\nSELECT toDecimal64(-12.647, 3) as a, toDecimal32(2.1239, 4) as b, multiplyDecimal(a, b)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─multiply(toDecimal64(-12.647, 3), toDecimal32(2.1239, 4))─┐\n│                                               -26.8609633 │\n└───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n┌───────a─┬──────b─┬─multiplyDecimal(toDecimal64(-12.647, 3), toDecimal32(2.1239, 4))─┐\n│ -12.647 │ 2.1239 │                                                         -26.8609 │\n└─────────┴────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n```sql\nSELECT\n    toDecimal64(-12.647987876, 9) AS a,\n    toDecimal64(123.967645643, 9) AS b,\n    multiplyDecimal(a, b)\n\nSELECT\n    toDecimal64(-12.647987876, 9) AS a,\n    toDecimal64(123.967645643, 9) AS b,\n    a * b\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─────────────a─┬─────────────b─┬─multiplyDecimal(toDecimal64(-12.647987876, 9), toDecimal64(123.967645643, 9))─┐\n│ -12.647987876 │ 123.967645643 │                                                               -1567.941279108 │\n└───────────────┴───────────────┴───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n\nReceived exception from server (version 22.11.1):\nCode: 407. DB::Exception: Received from localhost:9000. DB::Exception: Decimal math overflow: While processing toDecimal64(-12.647987876, 9) AS a, toDecimal64(123.967645643, 9) AS b, a * b. (DECIMAL_OVERFLOW)\n```\n\n## divideDecimal\n\nDivides two `Decimal` values, `a` by `b`. The result is a `Decimal256`. You can optionally specify the `result_scale` to control the precision of the output. If `result_scale` is not provided, the maximum scale of the input values is used. This function is slower than the standard `divide` function but offers precise control over decimal arithmetic.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\ndivideDecimal(a, b[, result_scale])\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The dividend. [`Decimal`](../data-types/decimal).\n- `b`: The divisor. [`Decimal`](../data-types/decimal).\n- `result_scale`: (Optional) The desired scale (number of decimal places) for the result. [`Int/UInt`](../data-types/int-uint).\n\n### Returns\n\nThe quotient of `a` divided by `b` with the specified or inferred scale. [`Decimal256`](../data-types/decimal).\n\n### Example\n\n```result\n┌─divideDecimal(toDecimal256(-12, 0), toDecimal32(2.1, 1), 10)─┐\n│                                                -5.7142857142 │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### Differences compared to regular division\n\n```sql\nSELECT toDecimal64(-12, 1) / toDecimal32(2.1, 1)\nSELECT toDecimal64(-12, 1) as a, toDecimal32(2.1, 1) as b, divideDecimal(a, b, 1), divideDecimal(a, b, 5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─divide(toDecimal64(-12, 1), toDecimal32(2.1, 1))─┐\n│                                             -5.7 │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n\n┌───a─┬───b─┬─divideDecimal(toDecimal64(-12, 1), toDecimal32(2.1, 1), 1)─┬─divideDecimal(toDecimal64(-12, 1), toDecimal32(2.1, 1), 5)─┐\n│ -12 │ 2.1 │                                                       -5.7 │                                                   -5.71428 │\n└─────┴─────┴────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┴────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n```sql\nSELECT toDecimal64(-12, 0) / toDecimal32(2.1, 1)\nSELECT toDecimal64(-12, 0) as a, toDecimal32(2.1, 1) as b, divideDecimal(a, b, 1), divideDecimal(a, b, 5)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\nDB::Exception: Decimal result's scale is less than argument's one: While processing toDecimal64(-12, 0) / toDecimal32(2.1, 1). (ARGUMENT_OUT_OF_BOUND)\n\n┌───a─┬───b─┬─divideDecimal(toDecimal64(-12, 0), toDecimal32(2.1, 1), 1)─┬─divideDecimal(toDecimal64(-12, 0), toDecimal32(2.1, 1), 5)─┐\n│ -12 │ 2.1 │                                                       -5.7 │                                                   -5.71428 │\n└─────┴─────┴────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┴────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## byteSwap\n\nReverses the byte order (endianness) of an integer value.\n\n### Syntax\n\n```sql\nbyteSwap(a)\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n- `a`: The integer value whose bytes are to be swapped.\n\n### Returns\n\nThe integer with its bytes reversed. The return type is the same as the input type.\n\n### Example\n\n```sql\nbyteSwap(3351772109)\n```\n\nResult:\n\n```result\n┌─byteSwap(3351772109)─┐\n│           3455829959 │\n└──────────────────────┘\n```\n\nThe previous example can be followed in the following manner:\n\n1. Convert the base-10 integer to its equivalent hexadecimal format in big-endian format, for example `3351772109 -\u003e C7 C7 FB CD (4 bytes)`.\n2. Reverse the bytes, for example `C7 C7 FB CD -\u003e CD FB C7 C7`.\n3. Convert the result back to an integer assuming big-endian, for example `CD FB C7 C7  -\u003e 3455829959`.\n\nA use case of this function is reversing IPv4s:\n\n```result\n┌─toIPv4(byteSwap(toUInt32(toIPv4('205.251.199.199'))))─┐\n│ 199.199.251.205                                       │\n└───────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"8:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative\",\"role\":\"main\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L20\",null,{\"pageContent\":\"$21\",\"pagePath\":\"app/__sql-reference/functions/arithmetic-functions\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"article\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":1,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Arithmetic functions\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":\"The following functions are used to perform arithmetic operations.\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":[\"Arithmetic functions work for any two operands of type \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"UInt8\"}],\", \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"UInt16\"}],\", \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"UInt32\"}],\", \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"UInt64\"}],\", \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"Int8\"}],\", \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"Int16\"}],\", \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"Int32\"}],\", \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"Int64\"}],\", \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"Float32\"}],\", or \",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"Float64\"}],\".\"]}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":\"Before performing the operation, both operands are cast to the result type.
